[2;36m                    [0m         [39m===Evaluation [0m[33mReport[0m[39m===[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA Jazzer fuzzer run detected a Server-Side Request Forgery [0m[1;39m([0m[39mSSRF[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m attempt when [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparsing an XFA resource in Apache PDFBox. The fuzzer-triggered code path led to an [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moutbound socket connection to “jazze.com:[0m[1;36m80[0m[39m,” which was flagged and blocked by [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mJazzer’s SSRF sanitizer [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`FuzzerSecurityIssueMedium`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. This indicates that [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39muntrusted input can drive network requests during XML parsing of XFA forms.[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Issue type: Server-Side Request Forgery [0m[1;39m([0m[39mSSRF[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Detection mechanism: [0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`com.code_intelligence.jazzer.sanitizers.ServerSideRequestForgery`  [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Trigger: During `[0m[1;35mPDXFAResource.getDocument[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, the XML parser resolves an [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexternal entity and attempts an HTTP connection.  [0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Stack trace highlights:[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - `ServerSideRequestForgery.checkSsrf` and `checkSsrfSocket` invoked before the [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msocket connect.[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - Core JDK networking calls [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`java.net.Socket.connect`, [0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`HttpURLConnection.connect`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m originate from Apache Xerces XML parsing.[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - Parsing entry point:  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    - `DomXfaParserFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput` →  [0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    - `PDXFAResource.getDocument` →  [0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    - `DocumentBuilder.parse` →  [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    - Xerces entity manager initiating an HTTP connection.[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mImportant observations and findings:[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The SSRF sanitizer intercepted an outbound connection based on untrusted data [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mthe parsed XML/XFA input[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The external HTTP request root is in the XML entity resolution flow of Xerces, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minvoked by PDFBox’s XFA form handling.[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The fuzzer harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`DomXfaParserFuzzer`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is only the entry point; the vulnerable[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbehavior lies in the XML parsing and XFA resource loading logic.[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mCode areas to investigate for a holistic understanding:[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. `com.example.DomXfaParserFuzzer` – the fuzzer harness invoking XFA parsing.[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. `org.apache.pdfbox.pdmodel.interactive.form.PDXFAResource.getDocument` – [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconversion of the XFA stream to a DOM `Document`.[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. XML parser configuration in PDFBox [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., `DocumentBuilderFactory` settings, [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexternal entity handling[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Underlying Apache Xerces entity resolution logic [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`XMLEntityManager`, [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`XMLDocumentFragmentScannerImpl`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m that triggers network requests.[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Any other PDFBox components handling XML-based form data [0m[1;39m([0m[39mto check for similar [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mSSRF risks[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
